    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
    </p>
    <h2>
     <a id="_1">
     </a>
     程序设计语言
    </h2>
    <p>
     机器语言：
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      一种二进制语言，它直接使用二进制代码表达指令，是计算机硬件可以直接识别和执行的程序设计语言
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     汇编语言：
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      使用方便记忆符与机器语言中的指令–对应
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     高级语言：
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      是接近自然语言的一种计算机程序设计语言，python、java都是高级语言
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     编程语言的分类：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      编译型
     </li>
     <li>
      解释型
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     编译型：是指将源代码转换成目标代码的过程，通常源代码是高级语言代码，目标代码是机器语言代码，执行编译的计算机程序称为编译器（compiler）
    </p>
    <p>
     解释型：是指将源代码逐条转换成目标代码同时逐条进行目标代码的过程，执行解释的计算机程序称之为解释器(interpreter)
    </p>
    <h2>
     <a id="print_19">
     </a>
     print用法
    </h2>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>输出内容<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>函数的完整的语法格式
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>value<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>sep<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">''</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'\n'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello world!!!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#编写程序</span>
a<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">100</span>  
b<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">50</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"欢迎大家!"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'bbbbb'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'aaaaaa'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token operator">+</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      写入文件
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">fp<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'note.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'w'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>   <span class="token comment">#打开文件w是写的意思</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'你好啊！'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token operator">=</span>fp<span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#将北京欢迎你输出到note.txt文件中</span>
fp<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#关闭文件</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      使用连接符，连接字符串
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"北京"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"--&gt;"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"欢迎你！"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#没有修改end符号，所以print结束之后有一个换行</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"北京欢迎你"</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token string">'2025'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#打印结果为北京欢迎你2025，没有换行</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="input_41">
     </a>
     input用法
    </h2>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">语法结构：
x<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'提示文字'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#无论输入的数据是什么，都是字符串类型</span>

a<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入你的名字:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#输入名字并且输出</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_49">
     </a>
     注释：
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      程序员在代码中对代码功能解释说明的标注性文字可以调高代码的可读性
      <br/>
      注释的内容被python解释器忽略，不被计算机执行单行注释，多行注释和中文声明注释。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_52">
     </a>
     代码缩进:
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      是指每行语句开始前的空白区域，用来表示python程序间 的包含和层次关系
      <br/>
      类定义，函数定义，流程控制语句，以及异常处理语句等行尾 的冒号和下一行的缩进表示一个代码块的开始，而缩进结束，则表示一个代码块的结束
      <br/>
      通常情况下采用个空格作为一个缩进量
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h2>
     <a id="python_56">
     </a>
     python中的数据类型和运算符
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_57">
     </a>
     保留字和标识符
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      在python中被赋予一些特定意义的一些单词，在开发程序的时候，不可以把这些保留字作为变量，函数，类，模块和其他对象名称来使用(保留字严格区分大小写)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> keyword
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>keyword<span class="token punctuation">.</span>kwlist<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#导入keyword保留字，之后查看保留字列表</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">len</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>keyword<span class="token punctuation">.</span>kwlist<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#统计保留字的个数        #len是python中的内置函数</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_64">
     </a>
     标识符的命名规则
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      python标识符可以是字符，数字，下划线，并且第一个字符不能是数字
      <br/>
      不能使用python中的保留字
      <br/>
      标识符严格区分大小写
      <br/>
      以下划线开头的标识符有着特殊的意义，一般应该避免使用相似的标识符，允许使用中文作为标识符，但是不建议使用
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="_69">
     </a>
     标识符的命名规范
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      模块名尽量短小，并且全部使用小写字母，可以使用下划线分割多个字母。例如：grame_main
      <br/>
      包名尽量短小，并且全部使用小写字母，不推荐使用下划线。例如:com.ysjpython,不推荐使用com_ysjpython
      <br/>
      类名采用单词首字母大写形式(Pascal风格)，例如:MyClass
      <br/>
      模块内部的类采用"
      <em>
       “+Pascal风格的类名组成，例如在MyClass中的内部_InnerMyClass
       <br/>
       函数，类的属性和方法的命名，全部使用小写字母，多个字母之间使用下划线分隔
       <br/>
       常量命名时采用全部大写字母，可以使用下划线
       <br/>
       使用单下划线”
      </em>
      "开头的模块变阿玲或者函数是受保护的，使用from xxx import *“语句从模块中导入的时候，这些模块变量或者函数不能被导入，使用双下划线”_"开头的实例变量或者方法是类私有的
      <br/>
      以双下划线开头和结尾的是python的专用标识，例如:
      <strong>
       init
      </strong>
      ()表示初始化函数
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_78">
     </a>
     变量的定义和使用
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      变量是保存和表示数据的值 的一种语法元素
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="_80">
     </a>
     变量的语法结构：
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      变量名=value
      <br/>
      luck_number=8
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">a<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">8</span>
b<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'a'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#使用type来查看数据类型是什么</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     在pyhton中允许多个变量指向同一个值
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">no<span class="token operator">=</span>number<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1023</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>no<span class="token punctuation">,</span>number<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>no<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>number<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_96">
     </a>
     变量的命名规则:
    </h4>
    <ul>
     <li>
      变量名必须是一个有效的标识符
     </li>
     <li>
      变量名不能使用python中的保留字
     </li>
     <li>
      谨慎使用小写字母i和大写字母o
     </li>
     <li>
      选择有意义的单词作为变量名
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h3>
     <a id="_101">
     </a>
     基本数据类型
    </h3>
    <p>
     1.整数类型
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      表示的数字是没有小数部分的数值,包含正整数,负整数和0
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     2.浮点型
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      表示带有小数点点数值,由整数部分和小数部分组成
      <br/>
      注意事项:两个浮点类型的数在进行运算的时候,有一定的概率运算结果增加一些不确定的尾数
      <br/>
      python中的复数与数学中的复数形式完全一致,由实部和虚部组成
      <br/>
      pyhton中的实数部分使用.real表示,虚数部分使用.imag表示
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0.1</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token number">0.2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">round</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0.1</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token number">0.2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#round可以定义保留的位数</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     3.字符串类型
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      连续的字符序列,可以表示计算机能识别的一切字符
      <br/>
      字符串的界定符:单引号,双引号,三引号
      <br/>
      原字符:使转移字符失效的字符,r或R
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code>info="""
收件人:韩子
手机号:111
"""
print(info)
三个引号将多个字符串包含,从而输出了多个字符串
</code></pre>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      字符串又称之为有序的字符序列,对于字符串中,某一个字符的检索,称之为索引
      <br/>
      对字符串中某个子串或者区间的检索称之为切片,切片的语法结构: 字符串或者字符串变量[n:m]
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'hello world~'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">len</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">12</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#取索引为0的,反向取索引为-12的</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'北京欢迎你'</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">7</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>           <span class="token comment">#从2-7不包含7</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#反向递减</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>           <span class="token comment">#默认是切到字符串的结尾</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>            <span class="token comment">#默认是从0开始切到4不包含5</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     4.布尔类型
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      用来表示真或者假,在python中使用标识符True或者False表示布尔类型的值
      <br/>
      True表示整数1,False表示整数0
      <br/>
      布尔值为False的情况如下
     </p>
     <p>
      False或者None
      <br/>
      数字中的0,包含0,0.0,虚数0
      <br/>
      空序列,包含空字符串、空元祖、空列表、空字典、空集合
      <br/>
      自定义对象的实例,该对象的__bool__()方法返回False或者__len__()方法返回0
     </p>
     <p>
      非0的整数的布尔值全是True
      <br/>
      所有非空字符串的布尔值都是True
      <br/>
      空字符串的布尔值为False
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="_156">
     </a>
     常用的字符串操作
    </h4>
    <p>
     1.x+y 将字符串x与y连接起来
     <br/>
     2.x
     <em>
      n或n
     </em>
     x 复制n次字符串x
     <br/>
     3.x in s 如果x时s的子串,结果为True,否则结果为False
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">x<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'2025'</span>
y<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'新的一年'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token operator">+</span>y<span class="token punctuation">)</span>          <span class="token comment">#结果是2025新的一年</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token operator">+</span>y<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">*</span><span class="token number">10</span> <span class="token punctuation">)</span>    <span class="token comment">#将这个内容复制10次</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'北京'</span><span class="token keyword">in</span> y<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    <span class="token comment">#判断在y中是否存在北京存在就是true否则就是false</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'上海'</span><span class="token keyword">in</span> y<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_168">
     </a>
     数据类型之间的相互转换
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      int(x) 吧x转换为整数类型
      <br/>
      float(x) 把x转换为浮点数类型
      <br/>
      str(x) 把x转换成字符串
      <br/>
      chr(x) 将整数x转换为一个字符
      <br/>
      ord(x) 讲一个字符x转换为其对应的整数值
      <br/>
      hex(x) 将一个字符x转换为一个十六进制字符串
      <br/>
      oct(x) 将一个整数x转换为一个八进制字符串
      <br/>
      bin(x) 将一个整数x转换成一个二进制字符串
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">x<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">10</span>
y<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">3</span>
z<span class="token operator">=</span>x<span class="token operator">/</span>y
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>z<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>z<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">int</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">3.22222</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
c<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">ord</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'韩'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>c<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">chr</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">26472</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#进制转换</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'十进制转换为二进制'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">hex</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">12345</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"十进制转换为八进制"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">oct</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">12345</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"十进制转换为二进制"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">bin</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">12345</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="eval_192">
     </a>
     eval()函数的使用
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      python中的内置函数
      <br/>
      用于去掉字符串最外侧的引号,并且按照python语句方式执行去掉引号后的字符串
      <br/>
      eval()函数通常和input()函数一起使用
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="eval_197">
     </a>
     eval的语法格式
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      变量=eval(字符串)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">hello<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'北京欢迎你!'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>hello<span class="token punctuation">)</span>                <span class="token comment">#直接输出</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>hello<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>            <span class="token comment">#输出类型</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>            <span class="token comment">#去掉''输出hallo函数</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'\'北京欢迎你!!\''</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#去掉引号输出北京欢迎你!!</span>

s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'3.14+3'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">int</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">int</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_209">
     </a>
     算术运算符
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <ul>
      <li>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <ul>
      <li>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <ul>
      <li>
       // 整除 % 取余
       <br/>
       ** 幂运算 运算符的优先级由高到低 第一级: ** 第二级: *、/、%、// 第三级: +、-
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <a id="_215">
      </a>
      赋值运算符
     </h2>
     <p>
      += /=
      <br/>
      *= %=
      <br/>
      **= //=
     </p>
     <p>
      关系运算符
      <br/>
      &lt;
      <br/>
      = &lt;=
      <br/>
      == !=
      <br/>
      逻辑运算符 and(从左到右结合) or(从左到右结合)
     </p>
     <p>
      not(从右到左结合)
     </p>
     <p>
      位运算符 &amp; 与运算(全1为1其余为0) | 或运算(全0为0其余为1) ^ 异或运算(全1为0,其余为1) ~
      <br/>
      取反运算(1为0,0为1)
     </p>
     <p>
      左移位(&lt;&lt;) 将一个二进制的数字向左移动指定的位数,左边(高位端)溢出的位数被丢弃,右边(低位端)的空位用0补充
     </p>
     <p>
      右移位(&gt;&gt;)
      <br/>
      是将一个二进制数向右移动指定的位数,右边(低位端)溢出的位卑丢弃,左边(高位端)的空位端,如果最高位是0(正数)左侧空位填0,如果最高位是1(负数),左侧空位填写1.
     </p>
     <p>
      左乘右除
     </p>
     <p>
      运算符的优先级
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token operator">*</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token operator">/</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token operator">//</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token operator">**</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

x<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">20</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span>            <span class="token comment">#20</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#int</span>
x<span class="token operator">+=</span>x
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span>            <span class="token comment">#40</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#int</span>
x<span class="token operator">/=</span>x
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span>            <span class="token comment">#1.0</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#float</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">int</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#1</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#float </span>

<span class="token comment">#链式赋值</span>
a<span class="token operator">=</span>b<span class="token operator">=</span>c<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">100</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">float</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token operator">+</span>b<span class="token operator">+</span>c<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>c<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>c<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#系列解包赋值</span>
a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span>
a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token operator">=</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>a
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span>         <span class="token comment">#值的交换,将a和b的值交换 a变成20,b变成10</span>

<span class="token comment">#比较运算符</span>
a<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">10</span>
b<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">20</span>
c<span class="token operator">=</span>a<span class="token operator">==</span>b
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>c<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token operator">&lt;</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#逻辑运算符的使用</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span> <span class="token boolean">False</span> <span class="token keyword">or</span> <span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token boolean">True</span> <span class="token keyword">and</span> <span class="token boolean">False</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token boolean">False</span> <span class="token keyword">and</span> <span class="token boolean">False</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token boolean">True</span> <span class="token keyword">or</span> <span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_288">
     </a>
     程序练习:
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">father_height<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入爸爸的身高:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
mother_height<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入妈妈的身高:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
son_height<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>father_height<span class="token operator">+</span>mother_height<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">*</span><span class="token number">0.54</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'儿子的身高为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>son_height<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'cm'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>


a<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入一个四位的整数:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'个位数为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'十位数为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token operator">//</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'百位数为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token operator">//</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'千位数为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token operator">//</span><span class="token number">1000</span><span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'-'</span><span class="token operator">*</span><span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

num<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入一个四位的整数:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'个位上的数字为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>num<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'十位上的数字为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>num<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'百位上的数字为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>num<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'千位上的数字为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>num<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'-'</span><span class="token operator">*</span><span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_311">
     </a>
     程序的描述方式
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_312">
     </a>
     自然语言
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      Input #输入
      <br/>
      Process #处理
      <br/>
      Output #输出
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_318">
     </a>
     顺序结构
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      按照程序语句的自然顺序,从上到下,依次执行每条语句程序
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     赋值语句
     <br/>
     输入/输出语句
     <br/>
     模块导入语句
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">name<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入您的姓名:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
age<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"请输入您的年龄:"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'姓名:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'年龄:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_330">
     </a>
     选择结构
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#if语句</span>
c<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入一个数字:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">if</span> c<span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>c<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'是偶数'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>c<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'是奇数'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
    
num<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入一个数字:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'中'</span><span class="token keyword">if</span> num<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'1234567'</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token string">'低'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>



多分支<span class="token keyword">if</span>语句

score<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入您的成绩:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">if</span> score<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token keyword">or</span> score<span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'不合格,请重新输入!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">elif</span> score<span class="token operator">&gt;=</span><span class="token number">90</span> <span class="token keyword">and</span> score<span class="token operator">&lt;=</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'合格'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">elif</span>   score<span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token number">50</span> <span class="token keyword">and</span> score<span class="token operator">&lt;=</span><span class="token number">60</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'及格'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'不及格'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
<span class="token keyword">if</span>嵌套的使用
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_360">
     </a>
     多个条件的连接
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      使用and连接多个条件判断时,只有同时满足多个条件,才能执行if语句
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">user_name<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入您的用户名:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
pwd<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入您的密码:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">if</span> user_name<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'hjm'</span> <span class="token keyword">and</span> pwd<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'888'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"登陆成功!"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"登陆失败"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_371">
     </a>
     循环结构
    </h3>
    <h4>
     <a id="for_372">
     </a>
     for循环
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#遍历字符串</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#range函数</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>        包含<span class="token number">0</span>不包含<span class="token number">10</span>的整数序列<span class="token number">0</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">9</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
<span class="token comment">#range函数</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">11</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> i<span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'是偶数'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>


<span class="token builtin">sum</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">101</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token builtin">sum</span><span class="token operator">+=</span>i
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">sum</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

三角形
 <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">6</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> j <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">6</span><span class="token operator">-</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">' '</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">''</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> k <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>i<span class="token operator">*</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'*'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">''</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> 
    
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="while_403">
     </a>
     while循环
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      4步骤:
      <br/>
      1)初始化变量
      <br/>
      2)条件判断
      <br/>
      3)语句块
      <br/>
      4)改变变量
     </p>
     <p>
      程序跳出语句break
      <br/>
      跳出循环结构,通常用if一起搭配使用
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">answer<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"今天需要上课吗?y/n"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">while</span> answer<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'y'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
     <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'好好学习天天向上'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
     answer <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"今天需要上课吗?y/n"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="break_420">
     </a>
     break使用
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">使用<span class="token keyword">for</span>循环
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    user_name<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入用户名:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    pwd<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入密码:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> user_name<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'hjm'</span> <span class="token keyword">and</span> pwd<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'aaa'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'系统正在登录,请稍后!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">break</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span>  i<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'还有'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token operator">-</span>i<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'次机会!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'三次均输入失败:!!!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

使用<span class="token keyword">while</span>循环
i<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span>
<span class="token keyword">while</span> i<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    user_name<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入用户名:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    pwd<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"请输入密码:"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> user_name<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'hjm'</span> <span class="token keyword">and</span> pwd<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'aaa'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
      <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'系统正在登录,请稍后!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
      <span class="token keyword">break</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> i<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'用户名或者密码不正确,您还有'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token operator">-</span>i<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'次机会'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    i<span class="token operator">+=</span><span class="token number">1</span>
<span class="token keyword">if</span> i<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'对不起,三次均输入失败,退出程序!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="pass_450">
     </a>
     空语句pass
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      pass是python中的保留字,在语法结构中只起到站位符的作用,是使语法结构完整,不报错
      <br/>
      一般情况可以在if、for、while、函数的定义、类的定义中使用
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#9*9 乘法表</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> j <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>i<span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>j<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token string">'*'</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token string">'='</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token operator">*</span>j<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'\t'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_462">
     </a>
     组合数据类型
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_463">
     </a>
     序列和索引
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      索引是一个用于存储多个值的连续空间,每个值都对应一个整数的编号,称之为索引
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'helloworld'</span>
<span class="token comment">#切片操作:</span>
s1<span class="token operator">=</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token comment">#索引从0开始,到5结束(不包含5)步长为2</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#省略开始位置,默认从0开始</span>
s2<span class="token operator">=</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#省略开始位置,省略步长</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#默认到结尾序列的最后一个元素(包含最后一个元素)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#11和12的代码功能相同</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#获取索引为0 2 4 8 的</span>
<span class="token comment">#步长为负数</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">11</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">#结果是一样的,将helloworld反向输出</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_484">
     </a>
     序列的相加操作
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      x in s #如果x时s的元素,结果为True,否则结果为False
      <br/>
      for not in s #如果x不是s的元素,结果为True,否则结果为False
      <br/>
      len(s) #序列s中的元素的个数(即序列的长度)
      <br/>
      mx(s) #序列s中的元素的最大值
      <br/>
      min(s) #序列s中元素的最小值
      <br/>
      s.index(x) #序列s中第一次出现元素x的位置
      <br/>
      s.count(x) #序列s中出现x的总次数
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'helloworld'</span>
a<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'e'</span> <span class="token keyword">in</span> s               <span class="token comment">#in的使用!</span>
b<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'e'</span> <span class="token keyword">not</span> <span class="token keyword">in</span> s           <span class="token comment">#not in的使用</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'e在helloworld中存在吗?'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'e在helloword中不存在吗?'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'len()'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">len</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#求长度</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'max()'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">max</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#最大值</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'min()'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">min</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#最小值</span>

<span class="token comment">#序列对象的方法,使用序列的名称去打点调用</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'s.index():'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>index<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>    <span class="token comment">#o在s.index第一次出现的索引的位置</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'s.count()'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>count<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>    <span class="token comment">#统计o在字符串s中出现的次数</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_507">
     </a>
     列表类型
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      是指一系列特定顺序的元素组成.是python中内置的可变序列
      <br/>
      在pyhton中使用[]定义列表,元素与元素之间使用英文的逗号分隔
      <br/>
      列表中的元素可以是任意的数据类型
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="_513">
     </a>
     列表创建的方法
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      使用[]直接创建列表
      <br/>
      语法结构:
      <br/>
      列表名=[element1,element2,…elementN]
      <br/>
      使用内置函数list()创建列表
      <br/>
      语法结构如下:
      <br/>
      列表名=list(序列)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'你好'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'world'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">98</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
lst2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">list</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'helloworld10098'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
lst3<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">list</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst3<span class="token punctuation">)</span>                 <span class="token comment">#从1开始到10结束,步长为2,不包含10</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token operator">+</span>lst3<span class="token operator">+</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token operator">*</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">len</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>count<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#统计o的个数</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>index<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#统计o在列表中第一次出现的位置</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_535">
     </a>
     列表的删除
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      语法结构如下:
      <br/>
      del 列表名
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">list4<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>list4<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">del</span> list4        <span class="token comment">#删除列表</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_545">
     </a>
     函数的使用:
    </h4>
    <p>
     enumerate函数的使用语法结构
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'world'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'python'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'php'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> lst<span class="token punctuation">:</span>        <span class="token comment">#使用for循环遍历列表</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">' '</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#使用for循环和range()函数,len()函数,根据索引进行遍历</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">len</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">' '</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#使用enumerate()函数</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>item <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">enumerate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>item<span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">' '</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#b是序号,不是索引</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">for</span> b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>item <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">enumerate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">,</span>start<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>   <span class="token comment">#使用start指定序号为1,所以从1开始打印</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>item<span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">' '</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
<span class="token keyword">for</span> b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>item <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">enumerate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>   <span class="token comment">#不使用start,直接使用数字也可以开始</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>item<span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">' '</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_571">
     </a>
     列表的相关操作
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      lst.append(x) 在列表lst最后增加一个元素
      <br/>
      lst.insert(index,x) 在列表中第index位置增加一个元素
      <br/>
      lst,clear() 清除列表lst中所有元素
      <br/>
      lst.pop(index) 将列表lst中第index位置的元素取出来,并且从列表中将其删除
      <br/>
      lst.remove(x) 将列表lst中出现的第一个元素x删除 lst.reverse(x) 将列表lst中的元素反转
      <br/>
      lst.copy() 拷贝列表lst中的所有元素,生成一个新的列表
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">test<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'world'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'python'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'原列表:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#输出原来列表的内存地址</span>
<span class="token comment">#增加元素的操作:</span>
test<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'sql'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'增加元素后:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#内存地址不变,可是增加了一个sql元素</span>
<span class="token comment">#插入元素,在指定的索引上插入</span>
test<span class="token punctuation">.</span>insert<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#在索引为1的位置上插入了元素,其他元素后撤</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#列表元素的删除</span>
test<span class="token punctuation">.</span>remove<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'world'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#将列表中的world元素删除</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#使用pop(index)根据索引移除元素,然后删除</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pop<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>              <span class="token comment">#先将索引为1的元素取出来,然后将其删除</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#列表的反向输出</span>
test<span class="token punctuation">.</span>reverse<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#反向输出,内存地址不变</span>

<span class="token comment">#列表的拷贝</span>
new_test<span class="token operator">=</span>test<span class="token punctuation">.</span>copy<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>new_test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>new_test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#复制之后,元素是相同的,内存地址发生了改变</span>

<span class="token comment">#列表元素的修改,使用索引来做修改</span>
test<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'mysql'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>                <span class="token comment">#根据索引修改元素的值,但是内存地址不变</span>
<span class="token comment"># 清除所有元素</span>
test<span class="token punctuation">.</span>clear<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#列表中的所有元素都没了,但是内存地址不变</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_612">
     </a>
     列表的排序
    </h4>
    <ul>
     <li>
      列表对象的sort方法
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">60</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">89</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'原列表'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#排序,默认是升序</span>
lst<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sort<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'升序后'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#排序,降序</span>
lst<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sort<span class="token punctuation">(</span>reverse<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
lst2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'Banbana'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'apple'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'Orange'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'cat'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'原列表:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#生序排序,先排大写,再排小写</span>
lst2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sort<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'升序'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#降序排列</span>
lst2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sort<span class="token punctuation">(</span>reverse<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
