<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'降序'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#忽略大小写进行比较</span>
lst2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sort<span class="token punctuation">(</span>key<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>lower<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'忽略大小写'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      内置函数sorted()
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">56</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">98</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">28</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'原列表:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#使用sorted排序,默认是升序</span>
asc_lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">sorted</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'原列表:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'升序排序'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>asc_lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#降序排序,将reverse改成true</span>
desc_lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">sorted</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">,</span>reverse<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'降序排序:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>desc_lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

lst2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'banana'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'apple'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'Cat'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'Orange'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'原列表:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#忽略大小写排序</span>
new_lst2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">sorted</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">,</span>key<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>lower<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'原列表:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'忽略大小写排序:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>new_lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_660">
     </a>
     使用列表生成式来生成列表
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">
<span class="token keyword">import</span> random
lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>i <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">11</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token operator">*</span>i <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">11</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#自动产生一个1-100之间的列表里有10个随机数</span>
lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>random<span class="token punctuation">.</span>randint<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">for</span> _ <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">11</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#从列表中选择符合条件的元素去组成新的列表</span>
lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>i <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> i<span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_678">
     </a>
     二维列表的创建
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'城市'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'环比'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'同比'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'北京'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">102</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">103</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'上海'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">104</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">504</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'深圳'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">39</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'二维列表为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#for循环遍历二维列表</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> row <span class="token keyword">in</span> lst<span class="token punctuation">:</span>  <span class="token comment">#遍历每一行</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> row<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'\t'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#列表生成式,用于生成一个4行5列的二维列表</span>
lst2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>j <span class="token keyword">for</span> j <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_698">
     </a>
     元组类型
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      是python中内置的不可变序列,在python中使用()定义元组,元素与元素之间使用英文的逗号分隔,元组中只有一个元素的时候,逗号也不能省略
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="2_701">
     </a>
     元组的创建方式有2种
    </h4>
    <ul>
     <li>
      使用()直接创建元组
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#使用小括号创建元组</span>
t<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'python'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'world'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      使用内置函数tuple()创建元组
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#使用内置函数 tuple()创建元组</span>
t<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">tuple</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'helloworld!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
t<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">tuple</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'10在元组中是否存在:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span> <span class="token keyword">in</span> t<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'10在元组中不存在:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span> <span class="token keyword">not</span> <span class="token keyword">in</span> t<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'最大值:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">max</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'最小值:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">min</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'t.conut'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>t<span class="token punctuation">.</span>count<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'t.index'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>t<span class="token punctuation">.</span>index<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#如果元组中只有1个元素:</span>
t<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#如果元组中只有1个元素,逗号不能删除</span>
y<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>y<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>y<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_729">
     </a>
     删除元组
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">del</span> 元组名

<span class="token comment">#元组的删除</span>
<span class="token keyword">del</span> t
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span>            <span class="token comment">#删除以后在输出就会报错了!</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_737">
     </a>
     元组的访问与遍历
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">t<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'python'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'world'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#根据索引访问元素</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
t2<span class="token operator">=</span>t<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>     <span class="token comment">#元组支持切片操作</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#元组的遍历</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> t<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'遍历元组'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#for + range()+len()</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">len</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'根据索引:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>i<span class="token punctuation">,</span>t<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#使用enumerate()</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> index<span class="token punctuation">,</span>item <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">enumerate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>index<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'----&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">for</span> index<span class="token punctuation">,</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">enumerate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">,</span>start<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">11</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>index<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'----&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> item<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_760">
     </a>
     元组生成式
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#元组生成式</span>
t<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment"># t=tuple(t)</span>
<span class="token comment"># print(t)</span>

<span class="token comment">#遍历</span>
<span class="token comment"># for item in t:</span>
<span class="token comment">#     print(item,end=' ')</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__next__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__next__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__next__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

t<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">tuple</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>t<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_778">
     </a>
     元组和列表的区别
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      元组: python中的不可变序列,无法实现添加、删除和修改元素等操作、支持切片访问元素、不支持修改操作、访问和处理速度快、可以作为字典的键
     </p>
     <p>
      列表:可变序列 append()、insert()、remove()、pop()等方法实现添加和删除列表元素
      <br/>
      支持切片访问和修改列表中的元素,访问和处理速度慢,不能作为字典的键
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_785">
     </a>
     字典类型
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      字典类型是根据一个信息查找另外一个信息的方式构成了“键值对”,它表示索引用的键和对应的值构成的成对关系
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="_789">
     </a>
     字典的创建方式
    </h4>
    <ul>
     <li>
      使用{}直接创建字典
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      d={key1:value,ke2:value…}
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      使用内置函数dict()创建字典
      <br/>
      1)通过映射函数创建字典
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      zip(lst1,lst2
     </p>
     <p>
      语法结构如下:
      <br/>
      dict(key1=value1,ke2=value2…
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#(1)创建字典</span>
d<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'cat'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'dog'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'pet'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'zoo'</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#当key相同的时候,value进行了覆盖</span>
<span class="token comment">#(2) zip函数</span>
lst1<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
lst2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'cat'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'dog'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'pet'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'zoo'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'car'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
aaaa<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">zip</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst1<span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>aaaa<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment"># print(list(aaaa))</span>
d<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">dict</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>aaaa<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#(3) 使用参数创建字典</span>
d<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">dict</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cat<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>dog<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#左边的是键(key),右边的是值(value)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

t<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>t<span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#t时key 10是value,元组是可以作为字典中的key</span>
lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token comment">#print({lst:10})     #这里会报错,可变数据类型不能作为键(key)</span>

<span class="token comment">#字典属于序列</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'max:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">max</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'min:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">min</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'len:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">len</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#字典的删除</span>
<span class="token keyword">del</span>  d
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#这里就会报错提示</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_833">
     </a>
     注意事项:
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      字典中的key是无序的
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="_837">
     </a>
     字典的取值
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      d[key]或者d.get(key)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      字典元素的遍历
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      遍历出key与value的元组
      <br/>
      分别遍历出key和value
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">d<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'world'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'python'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token comment">#访问字典中的元素</span>
<span class="token comment"># (1) 使用d[key]</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment"># (2) 使用d.get(key)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#二者之间是有区别的,如果key不存在,d[key]会报错,d.get(key)可以指定默认值</span>
<span class="token comment"># print(d['java'])  会报错,java不存在</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'java'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#提示一个none</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'java'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'不能存在'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#不会输出None,而是输出一个不存在</span>

<span class="token comment">#字典的遍历</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> a <span class="token keyword">in</span> d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>items<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#key=value组成的一个元素!</span>

<span class="token comment">#在使用for循环遍历的时候,分别获取key,value</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> key<span class="token punctuation">,</span>value <span class="token keyword">in</span> d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>items<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>key<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'---&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>value<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_866">
     </a>
     字典的相关操作方法
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      d.keys() 获取所有的key数据
      <br/>
      d.values() 获取所有的value数据
      <br/>
      d.pop(key,default) key存在获取相应的value,同时删除key-value对,否则获取默认值
      <br/>
      d.popitem() #随机从字典中取出一个key-value对,结果为元组类型,同时将该key-value从字典中删除
      <br/>
      d.clear() 清空字典中所有的key-value对
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"> <span class="token comment">#创建字典</span>
d<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token number">1001</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'李梅'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1002</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'王华'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1003</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'张峰'</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#向字典中添加元素</span>
d<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1004</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'张丽'</span>    <span class="token comment">#直接使用赋值运算向字典中添加元素</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#获取字典中的所有的key</span>
keys<span class="token operator">=</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>keys<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>keys<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">list</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>keys<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">tuple</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>keys<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#获取字典中的所有的value</span>
values<span class="token operator">=</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>values<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>values<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">list</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>values<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">tuple</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>values<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#如何将字典中数据转换成key-value的形式,以元组的方式进行展现</span>
lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">list</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>items<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_898">
     </a>
     字典的生成式
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> random
<span class="token comment">#字典生成式</span>
d<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>item<span class="token punctuation">:</span>random<span class="token punctuation">.</span>randint<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token keyword">for</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#创建两个列表</span>
lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1001</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1002</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1003</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
lst2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'成'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'王'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'李'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
d<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>key<span class="token punctuation">:</span>value <span class="token keyword">for</span> key<span class="token punctuation">,</span>value <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">zip</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst2<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_911">
     </a>
     集合类型
    </h2>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      python中的集合与数学中的集合的概念是一致的
      <br/>
      python中的集合是一个无需不重复的元素序列
      <br/>
      集合中只能存储不可变的数据类型
      <br/>
      在python中集合使用{}定义 与列表、字典一样,都是pyhton中的可变数据类型
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_918">
     </a>
     集合的创建与删除方法
    </h3>
    <ul>
     <li>
      使用{}直接创建集合
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      语法结构:
      <br/>
      s={a,b,c,…n}
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      使用内置函数set()创建集合
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      语法结构:
      <br/>
      s=set(可迭代对象)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      del直接删除
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      del 集合名
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#{}直接创建集合</span>
<span class="token keyword">from</span> random <span class="token keyword">import</span> randint

s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#集合中只能存储不可变数据类型</span>
<span class="token comment"># s={[10,20],[30,40]}</span>
<span class="token comment"># print(s)        #不能存放列表,这里直接报错了</span>

<span class="token comment">#使用set()创建集合</span>
s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#空集合 空集合 的布尔值是False</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>        <span class="token comment">#创建的是集合还是字典呢?</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#直接使用{}创创建的字典</span>

s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'helloworld'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#这样就是集合了</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>            <span class="token comment">#集合是无序的,并且是不重复的</span>

s2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

s3<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">set</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s3<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#集合属于序列的一种</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'max'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">max</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s3<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'min'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">min</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s3<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'len'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">len</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s3<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'9在集合中存在嘛?'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">9</span> <span class="token keyword">in</span> s3<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'9在集合中不存在吗?'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">9</span> <span class="token keyword">not</span> <span class="token keyword">in</span> s3<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#集合的删除操作:</span>
<span class="token keyword">del</span> s3
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s3<span class="token punctuation">)</span>           <span class="token comment">#报错没有定义</span>

A<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">50</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
B<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">50</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">88</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">76</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token comment">#交集操作</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>A<span class="token operator">&amp;</span>B<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#并集操作</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>A<span class="token operator">|</span>B<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#差集操作</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>A<span class="token operator">-</span>B<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#补集操作</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>A<span class="token operator">^</span>B<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_981">
     </a>
     集合的相关操作方法
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      s.add(x) 如果x不在集合s中,将x添加到集合s中
      <br/>
      s.remove(x) 如果x在集合中,将其删除,否则报错
      <br/>
      s.clear() 清除集合中的所有的元素
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">29</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">39</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token comment">#向集合中添加元素</span>
s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>add<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#删除集合中的元素</span>
s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>remove<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">29</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment"># #清空集合中的元素:</span>
<span class="token comment"># s.clear()</span>
<span class="token comment"># print(s)</span>

<span class="token comment">#集合的遍历操作:</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> s<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#使用enumerate()函数</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> index<span class="token punctuation">,</span>i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">enumerate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>index<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'---&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#集合的生成式</span>
s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>i <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>i <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> i<span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_1014">
     </a>
     列表、元组、字典、集合的区别
    </h2>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      列表list 可变序列 可重复 有序 []
      <br/>
      元组tuple 不可变序列 可重复 有序 ()
      <br/>
      字典dict 可变序列 key不可重复 value可重复 无序 {key:value}
      <br/>
      集合set 可变序列 不可重复 无序 {}
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h2>
     <a id="cswitch_1021">
     </a>
     结构模式匹配(相当于c语言中的switch)
    </h2>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">data<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入匹配的数据:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">match</span> data<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">case</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token string">'name'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'hjm'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'age'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'字典'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">case</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">39</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'列表'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">case</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'元组'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">case</span> <span class="token keyword">_</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'不成功'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="Python_1034">
     </a>
     Python中的字符串及正则表达式
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1035">
     </a>
     字符串的常用操作:
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      字符串是python中的不可变数据类型
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>lower<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  将<span class="token builtin">str</span>字符串全部转换为小写字母<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为一个新的字符串
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>upper<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>    将<span class="token builtin">str</span>字符串全部转换成大写字母<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为一个新的字符串
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>split<span class="token punctuation">(</span>sep<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> 吧<span class="token builtin">str</span>按照指定的分隔符sep进行分隔<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为列表类型
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>count<span class="token punctuation">(</span>sub<span class="token punctuation">)</span> 结果为sub这个字符串在<span class="token builtin">str</span>中出现的次数
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>find<span class="token punctuation">(</span>sub<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    查询sub这个字符串在<span class="token builtin">str</span>中是否存在<span class="token punctuation">,</span>如果不存在结果为<span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>如果存在<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为sub首次出现的索引
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>index<span class="token punctuation">(</span>sub<span class="token punctuation">)</span> 功能与find<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>相同<span class="token punctuation">,</span>区别主要是查询的子串sub不存在时<span class="token punctuation">,</span>程序报错
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>startwith<span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    查询字符串<span class="token builtin">str</span>是否以子串s开头
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>endswith<span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>     查询字符串<span class="token builtin">str</span>是否以子串s结尾 
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>replace<span class="token punctuation">(</span>old<span class="token punctuation">,</span>news<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    使用news替换字体字符串s中所有的old字符串<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果是一个新的字符串
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>center<span class="token punctuation">(</span>width<span class="token punctuation">.</span>fillchar<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    字符串<span class="token builtin">str</span>在制定的宽度范围内剧中<span class="token punctuation">,</span>可以使用fillchar进行台填充
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>join<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">iter</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        在<span class="token builtin">iter</span>中的每个元素后面都增加一个新的字符串<span class="token builtin">str</span>
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>strip<span class="token punctuation">(</span>chars<span class="token punctuation">)</span>      从字符串中去掉左侧和右侧chars中列出的字符串
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>lstrip<span class="token punctuation">(</span>chars<span class="token punctuation">)</span>     从字符串中去掉左侧chars中列出的字符串
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>rstrip<span class="token punctuation">(</span>chars<span class="token punctuation">)</span>     从字符串中去掉右侧chars中列出的字符串
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      示例
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"> s1<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'HelloWorld'</span>
s2<span class="token operator">=</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>lower<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
s3<span class="token operator">=</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>upper<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">,</span>s2<span class="token punctuation">,</span>s3<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'aa'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
email<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'aa@qq.com'</span>
lst<span class="token operator">=</span>email<span class="token punctuation">.</span>split<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'@'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'邮箱名'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'域名'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o的次数为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>count<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o的索引为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>index<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o的首次出现位置为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>find<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'p的首次出现位置为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>find<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'p'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#值为-1,-1为不存在</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'aa.py'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>endswith<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'.py'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'aa.py'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>startswith<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'aa'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'aaaaa'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'aa.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>startswith<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'.py'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'bbbbb'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> 
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'aa.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>endswith<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'.py'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'helloworld'</span>
s1<span class="token operator">=</span>s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>replace<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'o'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'a'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#将o替换为a  最后一个参数是替换次数,默认是全部替换 </span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'aa'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>center<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'*'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>         <span class="token comment">#在左右两侧都填充为*</span>
s1<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'    hello    world    '</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>strip<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#去掉字符串两侧的空格</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>lstrip<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#去掉字符串左侧的空格</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>rstrip<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#去掉字符串右侧的空格</span>
s2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'dl-helloworld'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>strip<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'ld'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#去掉指定的ld(dl也会被去除)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>lstrip<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'ld'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#去掉左侧的指定的字符</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>rstrip<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'ld'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#去掉右侧的指定的字符</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1085">
     </a>
     格式化字符串的三种方式:
    </h3>
    <ul>
     <li>
      占位符
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      %s:字符串格式
      <br/>
      %d:十进制整数格式
      <br/>
      %f:浮点数格式
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      f-string
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      python3.6中引入的格式字符串的方式,比{}表明被替换的字符
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      str.format()方法:
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      模版字符串.format(逗号分隔的参数)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">name<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'马冬梅'</span>
age<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">18</span>
kg<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">98.5</span>
<span class="token comment">#常规用法</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'姓名:%s,年龄:%d,体重:%.0f'</span><span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">,</span>kg<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#f-string</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f'姓名:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>name<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">,年龄:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>age<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">,体重:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>kg<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#使用字符串format方法</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'姓名:{0},年龄:{1},体重:{2}'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">,</span>kg<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#0,1,2和name age kg的索引相对应</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1110">
     </a>
     格式化字符串的详细格式
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      : 引导符号
      <br/>
      填充: 用于填充单个字符
      <br/>
      对齐方式: &lt;左对齐 &gt;右对齐 ^居中对齐
      <br/>
      宽度: 字符串的输出宽度
      <br/>
      , 数字的千分位分隔符
      <br/>
      . 精度:浮点数小数部分的精度或者数字串的最大输出长度
      <br/>
      类型: 整数类型b\d\o\x\X 浮点数类型:e\E\f%
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'helloworld'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'{0:*&lt;20}'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#字符串的显示宽度为20,左对齐,空白部分使用*填充</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'{0:*&gt;20}'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#字符串的显示宽度为20,右对齐,空白部分使用*填充</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'{0:*^20}'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#字符串的显示宽度为20,居中对齐,空白部分使用*填充</span>

<span class="token comment">#居中对齐还有center</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>center<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'*'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'aaa'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#千位分隔符</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"{0:,}"</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">987654321</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#每三位一个,</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'{0:.2f}'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">3.1415926</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#保留两位的浮点数</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'{0:.5}'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#规定显示长度为5位,只能显示前5位</span>

<span class="token comment">#整数类型</span>
a<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">425</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'二进制:{0:b}\n十进制:{0:d}\n十六进制:{0:x}\n八进制:{0:o}'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1136">
     </a>
     字符串的编码和解码
    </h3>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1137">
     </a>
     字符串编码:
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      将str类型转换成byte类型,需要使用到字符串的encode()方法
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      语法格式:
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      str.encode(encoding=‘utf-8’,errore=/strict/ignore/replace’)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1145">
     </a>
     字符串解码:
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      将byte类型转换成str类型,需要使用到byte类型的decode()方法
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      语法格式:
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      byte.decode(encoding=‘utf-8’,errors=‘strict/ignore/replace’)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'伟大的中国梦'</span>
<span class="token comment">#编码:</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>encode<span class="token punctuation">(</span>errors<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'replace'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#默认是utf-8</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>encode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'gbk'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>errors<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'replace'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1159">
     </a>
     数据的验证:
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isdigit<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#所有字符都是数字(阿拉伯数字)</span>
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isnumeric<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#所有字符都是数字</span>
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isalpha<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#所有字符都是字母(包含中文字符)</span>
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isalnum<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#所有字符都是数字或字母(包含中文字符)</span>
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>islower<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#所有字符都是小写</span>
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isupper<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#所有字符都是大写</span>
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>istitle<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#所有字符都是首字母大写</span>
<span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isspace<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#所有字符都是空白字符(\n、\t等)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     示例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'123'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isdigit<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'123'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isnumeric<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'一二三'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isdigit<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello你好'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isalpha<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello你好123'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isalpha<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello你好一二三'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>isalpha<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1179">
     </a>
     数据的处理:
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      使用str.join()方法进行拼接字符串
      <br/>
      直接拼接
      <br/>
      使用格式化字符进行拼接
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     拼接示例
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span>
a<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'world'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'  '</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>join<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>s<span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"  "</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>join<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>s<span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'python'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">' '</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'world'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"%s  %s"</span><span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'{0}  {1}'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_1195">
     </a>
     正则表达式
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1196">
     </a>
     元字符
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      具有特殊意义的专用字符,例如 ^和$分别表示匹配的开始和结束
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code>.  匹配任意字符(除\n)  
\w  匹配字母、数字、下划线
\W  匹配非字母、数字、下划线
\s  匹配任意空白字符
\S  匹配任意非空白字符
\d  匹配任意十进制数
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1208">
     </a>
     限定符
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      用于限定匹配的次数
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code>? 匹配前面的字符0次或者1次  
+ 匹配前面的字符1次或者多次
* 匹配前面的字符0次或者多次
{n}匹配前面的字符n次
{n,}匹配前面的字符最少n次
{n,m}匹配前面的字符最小n次,最多m次
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1220">
     </a>
     其他字符
    </h3>
    <pre><code>区间字符 []    匹配[]中所指定的字符
排除字符 ^     匹配不在[]中指定的字符
选择字符 |     用于匹配|左右的任意字符
转义字符       同python中的转义字符
分组()        改变限定符的作用
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="re_1228">
     </a>
     re模块
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      python中的内置模块,用于实现python中的正则表达式操作
     </p>
    </blockquote>
