    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>     <span class="token comment">#实例方法</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f"大家好,我叫:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">,我今年:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>age<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">岁"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#student继承Persion类:</span>
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Student</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Person<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>  <span class="token comment">#小括号中写父类</span>
    <span class="token comment">#初始化的方法:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">,</span>stuno<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token builtin">super</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>__init__<span class="token punctuation">(</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#调用父类的初始化方法,为name和age赋值</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>stuno <span class="token operator">=</span> stuno

<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Doctor</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Person<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">,</span>department<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token builtin">super</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>__init__<span class="token punctuation">(</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>department <span class="token operator">=</span> department


stu<span class="token operator">=</span>Student<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'韩子'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'1001'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
doctor<span class="token operator">=</span>Doctor<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'张x'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">32</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'外科'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

stu<span class="token punctuation">.</span>show<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
doctor<span class="token punctuation">.</span>show<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>


<span class="token comment">#多继承:</span>
    
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">FatherA</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>           <span class="token comment">#初始化方法</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token operator">=</span>name                 <span class="token comment">#实例属性</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">showA</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>                   <span class="token comment">#实例方法</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"这是父类A中的方法"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">FatherB</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>         <span class="token comment">#初始化方法</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token operator">=</span>age               <span class="token comment">#实例属性</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">showB</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>                <span class="token comment">#实例方法</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'这是父类b的方法'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Son</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>FatherA<span class="token punctuation">,</span>FatherB<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>                 <span class="token comment">#多继承,继承了多个父类</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">,</span>gender<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>     <span class="token comment">#这里需要调用两个父类的初始化方法</span>
    FatherA<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__init__<span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">)</span>             <span class="token comment">#使用父类的名称来区别</span>
    FatherB<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__init__<span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gender<span class="token operator">=</span>gender

son<span class="token operator">=</span>Son<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'韩子'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'男'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
son<span class="token punctuation">.</span>showA<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
son<span class="token punctuation">.</span>showB<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1853">
     </a>
     方法重写
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      子类继承了父类就拥有了父类中共有成员和受保护的成员 父类的方法并不能完全适合子类的需要求这个时候子类就可以重写父类的方法
      <br/>
      子类在重写父类方法时,要求方法的名称必须与父类方法的名称相同,在子类重写后的方法中,可以通过super().xxx()调用父类中的方法
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1857">
     </a>
     多态
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      多态是多种形态,即便不知道一个变量所引用的对象到底是什么类型,仍然可以通过这个变量调用对象的方法
      <br/>
      在程序运行过程中根据变量所引用的对象的数据类型,动态决定调用哪个对象中的方法
      <br/>
      python语言中的多态,根本不关心对象的数据类型,也不关心类之间是否存在继承关系,只关心对象的行为(方法).只要不同的类中有同名的方法,即可实现多态
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Person</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">eat</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'人吃五谷杂粮'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Cat</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">eat</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'猫喜欢吃鱼'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Dog</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">eat</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'狗喜欢吃骨头'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#三个类中都有一个同名的方法,eat</span>
<span class="token comment">#编写函数:</span>
<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">fun</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>obj<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>  <span class="token comment">#obj是函数的形参</span>
    obj<span class="token punctuation">.</span>eat<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#通过变量obj调用eat方法</span>

<span class="token comment">#创建3个类的对象</span>
per<span class="token operator">=</span>Person<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
cat<span class="token operator">=</span>Cat<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
dog<span class="token operator">=</span>Dog<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

fun<span class="token punctuation">(</span>per<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#python中的多态,不关心对象的数据类型,只关心对象是否具有同名方法</span>
fun<span class="token punctuation">(</span>cat<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
fun<span class="token punctuation">(</span>dog<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="object_1890">
     </a>
     object类
    </h2>
    <p>
     所有类直接或者间接的父类
     <br/>
     所有类都拥有object类的属性和方法
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token builtin">object</span>类中特殊的方法
__new__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>   由系统调用<span class="token punctuation">,</span>用于创建对象
__init__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  创建对象时手动调用<span class="token punctuation">,</span>用于初始化对象属性值
__str__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>   对象的描述<span class="token punctuation">,</span>返回值是<span class="token builtin">str</span>类型<span class="token punctuation">,</span>默认输出对象的内存地址
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Person</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name <span class="token operator">=</span> name
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>age <span class="token operator">=</span> age
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f'大家好,我叫:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">,我今年:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>age<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">岁'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>


per<span class="token operator">=</span>Person<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hjm'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#创建对象的时候会自动调用__init__方法</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">dir</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>per<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>per<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'aasfasf'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
per<span class="token punctuation">.</span>show<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Person</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name <span class="token operator">=</span> name
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>age <span class="token operator">=</span> age

    <span class="token comment">#方法重写</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__str__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token string">'这是一个人类,具有name和age两个实例属性'</span>
        
per<span class="token operator">=</span>Person<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hjm'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>per<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'aasfasf'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#这里就不是内存地址,而是__str__方法中的内容,直接输出对象名,实际上是调用了__str__方法</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>per<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__str__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#两个办法都可以</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1928">
     </a>
     特殊属性
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">obj<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__dict__              对象的属性字典
obj<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__class__             对象所属的类
<span class="token keyword">class</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>__bases__           类的父类元组
<span class="token keyword">class</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>__base__            类的父类
<span class="token keyword">class</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>__mro__             类的层次结构
<span class="token keyword">class</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>_subclasses__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     类的子类列表
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">A</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">pass</span>
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">B</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">pass</span>
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">C</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>A<span class="token punctuation">,</span>B<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name <span class="token operator">=</span> name
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>age <span class="token operator">=</span> age

a<span class="token operator">=</span>A<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
b<span class="token operator">=</span>B<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
c<span class="token operator">=</span>C<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'韩子'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">12</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"对象a的属性字典:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__dict__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"对象b的属性字典:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__dict__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"对象c的属性字典:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>c<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__dict__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"对象A所属的类:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>a<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__class__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"对象B所属的类:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__class__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"对象C所属的类:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>c<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__class__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"*"</span><span class="token operator">*</span><span class="token number">50</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>end<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'\n'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"\n"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'A类的父类元组:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>A<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__bases__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'B类的父类元组:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>B<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__bases__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'C类的父类元组:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>C<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__bases__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"\n"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'A类的父类元:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>A<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__base__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'B类的父类元:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>B<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__base__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'C类的父类元:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>C<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__base__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#如果继承了N多个父类,结果只能显示第一个父类</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'A类的层次结构:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>A<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__mro__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'B类的层次结构:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>B<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__mro__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'C类的层次结构:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>C<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__mro__<span class="token punctuation">)</span>     <span class="token comment">#C类首先继承了A,B类,间接继承了Object类</span>

<span class="token comment">#子类列表:</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"A类的子类列表:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>A<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__subclasses__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#A的子类是C类</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"B类的子类列表:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>B<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__subclasses__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"C类的子类列表:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>C<span class="token punctuation">.</span>__subclasses__<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#无子类,空列表 </span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_1981">
     </a>
     类的深拷贝和浅拷贝
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1982">
     </a>
     变量的赋值
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      只是形成两个变量,实际上还是指向同一个对象
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1986">
     </a>
     浅拷贝
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      拷贝时,对象包含的子对象内容不拷贝,因此,源对象与拷贝对象会引用同一个子对象
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_1990">
     </a>
     深拷贝
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      使用copy模块的deepcopy函数,递归拷贝对象中包含的子对象,源对象和拷贝对象所有的子对象也不相同
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     类实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#使用类来求圆的面积以及周长</span>
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Circle</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>r<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>r <span class="token operator">=</span> r

    <span class="token comment">#计算面积的方法:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">get_area</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
     <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token number">3.14</span><span class="token operator">*</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>r<span class="token operator">*</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>r

    <span class="token comment">#计算周长的方法:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">get_zhouhcang</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token operator">*</span><span class="token number">3.14</span><span class="token operator">*</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>r

<span class="token comment">#创建对象:</span>
b<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"请输入圆的半径:"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
c<span class="token operator">=</span>Circle<span class="token punctuation">(</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#调用类里面的方法:</span>
mianji<span class="token operator">=</span>c<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get_area<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
zhouchang<span class="token operator">=</span>c<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get_zhouhcang<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f'圆的面积为:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>mianji<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f'圆的周长为:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>zhouchang<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#定义学生类录入5个学生信息存储到列表中</span>
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Stuendet</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token comment">#初始化的方法(self.是实例属性)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>age<span class="token punctuation">,</span>gender<span class="token punctuation">,</span>score<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token operator">=</span>name
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>age<span class="token operator">=</span>age
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gender<span class="token operator">=</span>gender
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>score<span class="token operator">=</span>score        <span class="token comment">#给实例属性赋值</span>

    <span class="token comment">#实例方法:  用于输出信息</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">info</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>age<span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gender<span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>score<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#开始创建对象:</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"请输入5位学生信息:(姓名#年龄#性别#成绩#:"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">6</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f'请输入第</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>i<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">位学生信息以及成绩:'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    s_lst<span class="token operator">=</span>s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>split<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'#'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#索引为0的是姓名,索引为1的是年龄,索引为2的是性别,索引为3的是成绩</span>
    <span class="token comment">#创建学生对象</span>
    stu<span class="token operator">=</span>Stuendet<span class="token punctuation">(</span>s_lst<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s_lst<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s_lst<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s_lst<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">#将学生对象添加到列表中</span>
    lst<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>stu<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#遍历列表,调用学生对象的info方法:</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> lst<span class="token punctuation">:</span>  <span class="token comment">#i的数据类型是student类型</span>
    i<span class="token punctuation">.</span>info<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">
<span class="token comment">#使用面向对象的思想实现乐器的弹奏:</span>
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Instrument</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
 <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">make_sound</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
     <span class="token keyword">pass</span>
     
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Erhu</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Instrument<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
 <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">make_sound</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
     <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"二胡在弹奏"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>            <span class="token comment">#对象的重写</span>
     
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Piano</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Instrument<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
 <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">make_sound</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
     <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"钢琴在弹奏"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
     
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Violin</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Instrument<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
 <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">make_sound</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
     <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"小提琴在弹奏"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#编写一个函数:</span>
<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">play</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
 a<span class="token punctuation">.</span>make_sound<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#创建对象</span>
erhu<span class="token operator">=</span>Erhu<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
paino<span class="token operator">=</span>Piano<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
Violin<span class="token operator">=</span>Violin<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#调用方法:</span>
play<span class="token punctuation">(</span>erhu<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
play<span class="token punctuation">(</span>paino<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
play<span class="token punctuation">(</span>Violin<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     子类父类,重写:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#使用面向对象的思想,设计自定义类:描述出租车和家用车的信息:</span>
<span class="token comment">#父类:</span>
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">fulei</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>chexing<span class="token punctuation">,</span>chepai<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>chexing <span class="token operator">=</span> chexing
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>chepai <span class="token operator">=</span> chepai
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">kaishi</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"我能启动"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">tingzhi</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"我能停止"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#子类:</span>
<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Chuzhuce</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fulei<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>chexing<span class="token punctuation">,</span>chepai<span class="token punctuation">,</span>gongsi<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token builtin">super</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>__init__<span class="token punctuation">(</span>chexing<span class="token punctuation">,</span>chepai<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#调用父类的初始化方法,给他们赋值</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gongsi <span class="token operator">=</span> gongsi                    <span class="token comment">#给自己的独有属性赋值</span>
    <span class="token comment">#重写父类的启动停止方法:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">kaishi</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"乘客您好!!"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f'我是</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gongsi<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">出租车公司,我的车牌是:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>chepai<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">,您要去哪里?'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">tingzhi</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"目的地到了,请您扫码付款,欢迎下次乘坐!"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>


<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Jiayongche</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fulei<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>chexing<span class="token punctuation">,</span>chepai<span class="token punctuation">,</span>xingming<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token builtin">super</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>__init__<span class="token punctuation">(</span>chexing<span class="token punctuation">,</span>chepai<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>xingming <span class="token operator">=</span> xingming

    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">kaishi</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"乘客您好!!"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f'我是</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>xingming<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">,我的车牌是:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>chepai<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">,我的轿车我做主?'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">tingzhi</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"到达目的地了,快去玩儿吧!!"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#对象创建:</span>
chuzuche<span class="token operator">=</span>Chuzhuce<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'上海大众迈腾'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'京A666666'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'字节跳动'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
chuzuche<span class="token punctuation">.</span>kaishi<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
chuzuche<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tingzhi<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>


sijiazhe<span class="token operator">=</span>Jiayongche<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'红旗'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'家AAAAAAA'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'韩子'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
sijiazhe<span class="token punctuation">.</span>kaishi<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
sijiazhe<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tingzhi<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2127">
     </a>
     模块
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2128">
     </a>
     简介
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      在python中的一个后缀名为.py的python文件就是一个模块
      <br/>
      模块中可以定义函数,类等
      <br/>
      模块也可以避免函数、类、变量等名称相互冲突的问题
      <br/>
      模块不仅提高了代码的可维护性,同时还提高了代码的可重用性
      <br/>
      在给模块命名的时候要求全部使用小写字母,多个单词之间使用下划线进行分隔
      <br/>
      如果自定义模块名称与系统内置模块名称相同,那么在导入的时候会优先的导入自定义的模块
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2137">
     </a>
     分类:
    </h3>
    <p>
     系统内置模块:
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      有开发人员编写好的模块,在安装python解释器时一同安装成计算机
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     自定义模块:
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      一个以.py结尾的文件就是一个模块,新建python问津,实际上就是新建模块
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     自定义模块的作用:
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      一是规范代码,将功能相同的函数,类等封装到一个模块中,让代码更易读,另外一个目的与系统内置模块相同,即可以背起她模块调用,提高开发效率.
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2150">
     </a>
     模块的导入:
    </h3>
    <p>
     模块编写完成就可以被其他模块进行调用,并且使用被调用模块中的功能
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span>导入方式的语法结构<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">import</span>模块名称 <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token keyword">as</span> 别名<span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span> <span class="token keyword">import</span>导入方式的语法结构<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">from</span> 模块名称 <span class="token keyword">import</span> 变量<span class="token operator">/</span>函数<span class="token operator">/</span>类<span class="token operator">/</span><span class="token operator">*</span>
    
后导入的模块会将之前导入的模块进行一个覆盖
</code></pre>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">from</span> my_name <span class="token keyword">import</span> info
info<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">import</span> my_name <span class="token keyword">as</span> a 


<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
a<span class="token punctuation">.</span>info<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2170">
     </a>
     包
    </h2>
    <p>
     含有__init__.py的文件或者文件夹
     <br/>
     可以避免模块名称相冲突的问题
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">使用<span class="token keyword">import</span> 包名<span class="token punctuation">.</span>模块名   导入
包被导入的时候__init__<span class="token punctuation">.</span>py中的文件的代码会自动的导入执行
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2179">
     </a>
     主程序运行:
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">if__name__<span class="token operator">==</span> <span class="token string">' __main__'</span> <span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">pass</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2186">
     </a>
     常用的内置模块
    </h2>
    <p>
     在安装python解释器与解释器一起安装进来的模块被称为系统内置模块,也称为标准模块或者标准库
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      os模块:与操作系统和文件相关操作有关的模块
      <br/>
      re模块:用于在Python的字符串中执行正则表达式的模块
      <br/>
      random模块:用于产生随机数的模块
      <br/>
      json模块:用于对高维数据进行编码和解码的模块
      <br/>
      time模块:与时间相关的模块
      <br/>
      datetime模块:与日期相关的模块,可以方便的显示日期并且对日期进行运算
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="random_2196">
     </a>
     random模块:
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      用于产生随机数的标准库
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">seed<span class="token punctuation">(</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    初始化给定的随机数种子<span class="token punctuation">,</span>默认为当前系统时间
random<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>    产生一个<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>之间的随机小数
randint<span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span> 生成一个<span class="token punctuation">[</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">]</span>之间的整数
randrange<span class="token punctuation">(</span>m<span class="token punctuation">,</span>n<span class="token punctuation">,</span>k<span class="token punctuation">)</span> 生成一个<span class="token punctuation">[</span>m<span class="token punctuation">,</span>n<span class="token punctuation">]</span>之步长为k的随机整数
uniform<span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span> 生成一个<span class="token punctuation">[</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">]</span>之间的随机小数
choice<span class="token punctuation">(</span>seq<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    从序列中随机选择一个元素
shuffle<span class="token punctuation">(</span>seq<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    将序列seq中元素随机排列<span class="token punctuation">,</span>返回打乱后的序列
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> random
<span class="token comment">#设置随机数种子</span>
random<span class="token punctuation">.</span>seed<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>random<span class="token punctuation">.</span>random<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>random<span class="token punctuation">.</span>randint<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span>  i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>random<span class="token punctuation">.</span>randrange<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="time_2223">
     </a>
     time模块:
    </h3>
    <p>
     time模块是python中提供的用于处理时间的标准库,可以用来进行时间处理,时间格式化和计时等
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">time<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>                获取当前时间戳
localtime<span class="token punctuation">(</span>sec<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        获取指定时间戳对应的本地时间的struct_time对象
ctime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>               获取当前时间戳对应的易读字符串
strftime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>            格式化时间<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为字符串
strptime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>            提取字符串的时间<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为struct_time对象
sleep<span class="token punctuation">(</span>sec<span class="token punctuation">)</span>            休眠sec秒

<span class="token operator">%</span>Y        年份         <span class="token number">0001</span><span class="token operator">~</span><span class="token number">9999</span>
<span class="token operator">%</span>m        月份         <span class="token number">01</span><span class="token operator">~</span><span class="token number">12</span>
<span class="token operator">%</span>B        月名         January<span class="token operator">~</span>December
<span class="token operator">%</span>d        日期         <span class="token number">01</span><span class="token operator">~</span><span class="token number">31</span>
<span class="token operator">%</span>A        星期         Monday<span class="token operator">~</span>Sunday
<span class="token operator">%</span>H        小时<span class="token punctuation">(</span>24h制<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token number">00</span><span class="token operator">~</span><span class="token number">23</span>
<span class="token operator">%</span>I        小时<span class="token punctuation">(</span>12h制<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token number">01</span><span class="token operator">~</span><span class="token number">12</span>
<span class="token operator">%</span>M        分钟         <span class="token number">00</span><span class="token operator">~</span><span class="token number">59</span>
<span class="token operator">%</span>s        秒           <span class="token number">00</span><span class="token operator">~</span><span class="token number">59</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> time
a<span class="token operator">=</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>time<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

b<span class="token operator">=</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>localtime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
c<span class="token operator">=</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ctime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>c<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

d<span class="token operator">=</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>localtime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">60</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#60表示60秒  默认的时间是1970.1.1.8时1分</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'年份:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tm_year<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'月份:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tm_mon<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'日期:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tm_mday<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'时:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tm_hour<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'分:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tm_min<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'秒:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tm_sec<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'星期:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tm_wday<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'今年的多少天:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tm_yday<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ctime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#获取当前时间,简单易读的字符串</span>


<span class="token comment">#日期时间格式化:</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>strftime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"%Y-%m-%d"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>localtime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#转换成年月日的表示方式:2025-01-18</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>strftime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"%H:%M:%S"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>localtime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#转换成时分秒表示方式:17:57:41</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'月份的名称:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>strftime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"%B"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>localtime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'星期的名称:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>strftime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"%A"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>localtime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>


time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sleep<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       <span class="token comment">#程序暂停2秒然后打印hello world</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello world'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="datetime_2273">
     </a>
     datetime模块
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      datetime模块可以更方便的显示日期并且对日期进行运算
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">datetime<span class="token punctuation">.</span>datetime        <span class="token comment">#表示日期时间的类</span>
datetime<span class="token punctuation">.</span>timedelta       <span class="token comment">#表示时间间隔的类</span>
datetime<span class="token punctuation">.</span>date            <span class="token comment">#表示日期的类</span>
datetime<span class="token punctuation">.</span>time            <span class="token comment">#表示时间的类</span>
datetime<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tzinfo          <span class="token comment">#时区相关的类</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">from</span> datetime <span class="token keyword">import</span> datetime
dt<span class="token operator">=</span>datetime<span class="token punctuation">.</span>now<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#这个模块是 获取当前的系统时间</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'当前的系统时间为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>dt<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#字符串类型转换成datetime类型:</span>
str_datetime<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'2028年5月1日20点20分'</span>

dt3<span class="token operator">=</span>datetime<span class="token punctuation">.</span>strptime<span class="token punctuation">(</span>str_datetime<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'%Y年%m月%d日  %H点%M分'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dt3<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>dt3<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     timedelta类的使用:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">from</span> datetime <span class="token keyword">import</span> datetime
<span class="token keyword">from</span> datetime <span class="token keyword">import</span> timedelta
<span class="token comment">#创建2个datetime类型的对象:</span>
delta1<span class="token operator">=</span>datetime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2028</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">-</span>datetime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2028</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'delta1的数据类型是:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>delta1<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'delta1'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>delta1<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"2028年5月1日之后的153天是:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>datetime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2028</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">+</span>delta1<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#通过传入参数的方式创建一个timedelta对象</span>
dt1<span class="token operator">=</span>timedelta<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"创建一个10天的timedelta对象"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>dt1<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

dt2<span class="token operator">=</span>timedelta<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"创建一个10天10秒的timedelta对象"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>dt2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2313">
     </a>
     第三方模块
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2314">
     </a>
     安装与卸载
    </h3>
    <p>
     第三方模块有全球python爱好者,程序员以及各行各业的专家进行开发并且进行维护
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="_2316">
     </a>
     语法:
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">安装
pip install  模块名称  
卸载
pip uninstall 模块名称
升级pip命令的语句结构<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
python <span class="token operator">-</span>m pip install <span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token operator">-</span>upgrade pip  <span class="token comment">#升级的语法</span>
pip insatll 模块名 <span class="token operator">-</span>i
http<span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token operator">//</span>pypi<span class="token punctuation">.</span>douban<span class="token punctuation">.</span>com<span class="token operator">/</span>simple <span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token operator">-</span>trusted<span class="token operator">-</span>host pypi<span class="token punctuation">.</span>douban<span class="token punctuation">.</span>com

pip install requests
pip uninstall requests
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2332">
     </a>
     常用的第三方模块
    </h2>
    <p>
     被称之为requests库,用于处理HTTP请求的第三方库,该库在爬虫程序中应用非常广泛.使用requests库中的get()函数可以打开一个网络请求,并且获取一个Response响应对象.响应结果中的字符串数据可以通过响应对象的text属性获取,响应结果中除了有字符串数据也有二进制数据,响应结果中的二进制数据可以通过响应对象的content属性获取
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="Requests_2334">
     </a>
     Requests模块的使用:(爬虫)
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span>  requests
<span class="token keyword">import</span>  re
url<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'https://www.weather.com.cn/weather1d/101010100.shtml'</span>  <span class="token comment">#用爬虫打开的浏览器上的网页</span>
response<span class="token operator">=</span>requests<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span>url<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#打开浏览器并且打开网址:</span>
<span class="token comment">#这里设置一下编码格式:</span>
response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>text<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#响应对象的text属性,使用对象名.属性名  response.text是属性 这里通过爬虫获得的是html页面</span>

city<span class="token operator">=</span>re<span class="token punctuation">.</span>findall<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'&lt;span class="name"&gt;([\u4e00-\u9fa5]*)&lt;/span&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>text<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
weather<span class="token operator">=</span>re<span class="token punctuation">.</span>findall<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'&lt;span class="weather"&gt;([\u4e00-\u9fa5]*)&lt;/span&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>text<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
wd<span class="token operator">=</span>re<span class="token punctuation">.</span>findall<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'&lt;span class="wd"&gt;(.*)&lt;/span&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>text<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
zs<span class="token operator">=</span>re<span class="token punctuation">.</span>findall<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'&lt;span class="zs"&gt;([\u4e00-\u9fa5]*)&lt;/span&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>text<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#print('城市为:',city)</span>
<span class="token comment"># print('指数为:',zs)</span>
<span class="token comment"># print('天气为:',weather)</span>
<span class="token comment"># print('气温为:',wd)</span>
lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>c<span class="token punctuation">,</span>d <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">zip</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>city<span class="token punctuation">,</span>weather<span class="token punctuation">,</span>zs<span class="token punctuation">,</span>wd<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    lst<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>c<span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">for</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> lst<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token triple-quoted-string string">'''
&lt;span class="wd"&gt;28/15℃&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span class="zs"&gt;适宜&lt;/span&gt;
'''</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     使用爬虫爬取百度logo
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> requests

url<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'https://www.baidu.com/img/PCtm_d9c8750bed0b3c7d089fa7d55720d6cf.png"'</span>
response<span class="token operator">=</span>requests<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span>url<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'logo.png'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'wb'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span>response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>content<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    ```
<span class="token comment">## 常用的第三方模块</span>
<span class="token operator">-</span> poenpyxl

<span class="token operator">&gt;</span> openpyxl模块是用于处理Microsoft Excel文件的第三方库 
<span class="token operator">&gt;</span> 可以对Excel文件中的数据进行写入和读取

```python
load_wordbook<span class="token punctuation">(</span>filename<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        打开已存在的表格<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为工作簿对象
workbook<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sheetnames            工作簿对戏那个的sheetnames属性<span class="token punctuation">,</span>用于获取所有工作表的名称<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为列表类型
sheet<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>              向工作表中添加一行数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>新数据接在工作表
workbook<span class="token punctuation">.</span>save<span class="token punctuation">(</span>excelname<span class="token punctuation">)</span>       保存工作簿
Workbook<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>                     创建新的工作簿对象
</code></pre>
    <p>
     pachong.py
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span>  requests
<span class="token keyword">import</span>  re

<span class="token comment">#自定义函数:</span>
<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">get_html</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>

    url<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'https://www.weather.com.cn/weather1d/101010100.shtml'</span>  <span class="token comment">#用爬虫打开的浏览器上的网页</span>
    response<span class="token operator">=</span>requests<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span>url<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#打开浏览器并且打开网址:</span>
<span class="token comment">#这里设置一下编码格式:</span>
    response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span>
<span class="token comment"># print(response.text)        #响应对象的text属性,使用对象名.属性名  response.text是属性 这里通过爬虫获得的是html页面</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> response<span class="token punctuation">.</span>text

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">pares_html</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>html_str<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    city<span class="token operator">=</span>re<span class="token punctuation">.</span>findall<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'&lt;span class="name"&gt;([\u4e00-\u9fa5]*)&lt;/span&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>html_str<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    weather<span class="token operator">=</span>re<span class="token punctuation">.</span>findall<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'&lt;span class="weather"&gt;([\u4e00-\u9fa5]*)&lt;/span&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>html_str<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    wd<span class="token operator">=</span>re<span class="token punctuation">.</span>findall<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'&lt;span class="wd"&gt;(.*)&lt;/span&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>html_str<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    zs<span class="token operator">=</span>re<span class="token punctuation">.</span>findall<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'&lt;span class="zs"&gt;([\u4e00-\u9fa5]*)&lt;/span&gt;'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>html_str<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#print('城市为:',city)</span>
<span class="token comment"># print('指数为:',zs)</span>
<span class="token comment"># print('天气为:',weather)</span>
<span class="token comment"># print('气温为:',wd)</span>
    lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>c<span class="token punctuation">,</span>d <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">zip</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>city<span class="token punctuation">,</span>weather<span class="token punctuation">,</span>zs<span class="token punctuation">,</span>wd<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        lst<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>a<span class="token punctuation">,</span>b<span class="token punctuation">,</span>c<span class="token punctuation">,</span>d<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    <span class="token keyword">return</span> lst
    ```
    ```python
<span class="token keyword">import</span> pachong
<span class="token keyword">import</span> openpyxl
html<span class="token operator">=</span>pachong<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get_html<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
lst<span class="token operator">=</span>pachong<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pares_html<span class="token punctuation">(</span>html<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#创建一个新的excel工作簿</span>
workbook <span class="token operator">=</span> openpyxl<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Workbook<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#创建对象</span>
<span class="token comment">#文件中创建工作表</span>
sheet <span class="token operator">=</span> workbook<span class="token punctuation">.</span>create_sheet<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'景区天气'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#向工作表中添加数据</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> lst<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    sheet<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
workbook<span class="token punctuation">.</span>save<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'景区天气.xlsx'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      pdfplumber可用于从PDf文件中读取内容
      <br/>
      Numpy 是python数据分析方向和其他库的依赖库,用于处理数组、矩阵等数据
      <br/>
      Pandas是基于Numpy扩展的一个非常重要的数据分析模块,使用Pandas读取Excel数据更加的方便
      <br/>
      Matplotlib是用于数据可视化的模块,使用Matplotlib.pyplot可以非常烦拜年的绘制饼图,柱形图,折线图等
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h2>
     <a id="IO_2440">
     </a>
     文件及IO操作
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2441">
     </a>
     文件
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      存储在计算机的存储设备中的一组数据序列就是文件 不同类型的文件通过后缀名进行区分
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2445">
     </a>
     文件的基本操作
    </h3>
    <p>
     1.打开文件
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      变量名=open(filename,mode,encoding)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     2.操作文件
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      变量名.read()
      <br/>
      变量名.write(s)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     3.关闭文件
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      变量名.close()
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">my_write</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
