    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'a.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'w'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'伟大的中国梦!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">my_read</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'a.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'r'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>read<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>close

<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    my_write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#调用函数</span>
    my_read<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_2474">
     </a>
     文件的打开模式:
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">r   以只读方式打开<span class="token punctuation">,</span>文件指针在文件的开头<span class="token punctuation">,</span>如果文件不存在<span class="token punctuation">,</span>程序抛异常
rb  以只读方式打开二进制文件<span class="token punctuation">,</span>如图片文件
w   覆盖写模式<span class="token punctuation">,</span>文件不存在创建<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>文件存在则内容覆盖
wb  覆盖写模式写入二进制数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>文件不存在则创建<span class="token punctuation">,</span>文件存在则覆盖
a   追加写模式<span class="token punctuation">,</span>文件不存在创建<span class="token punctuation">,</span>文件存在<span class="token punctuation">,</span>则在文件最后追加内容
<span class="token operator">+</span>   与w<span class="token operator">/</span>r<span class="token operator">/</span>a等一同使用<span class="token punctuation">,</span>在原功能的基础上增加同时读写功能
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_2483">
     </a>
     文件的读写方法:
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>read<span class="token punctuation">(</span>size<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        从文件中对size个字符或者字节<span class="token punctuation">,</span>如果没有给定参数<span class="token punctuation">,</span>则读区文件中的全部内容
<span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>readline<span class="token punctuation">(</span>size<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    读取文件中的一行数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>如果给定参数<span class="token punctuation">,</span>则为读取这一行中的size个字符或者字节
<span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>readlines<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       从文件中读取所有内容<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为列表类型 
<span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>          将字符串s写入文件
<span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>writelines<span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>   将内容全部为字符串的列表lst写入文件
<span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>seek<span class="token punctuation">(</span>offset<span class="token punctuation">)</span>      改变当前文件操作指针的位置<span class="token punctuation">,</span>英文占用一个字节<span class="token punctuation">,</span>中文gbk编码占用<span class="token number">2</span>个字节<span class="token punctuation">,</span>ut f<span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">8</span>占用<span class="token number">3</span>个字节
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">my_write</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token comment">#创建文件(打开)文件</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'a.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'a'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">#写入内容: </span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"\n"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">my_write_list</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    f<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'a'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    f<span class="token punctuation">.</span>writelines<span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    f<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> 


<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__ <span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    my_write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"伟大的中国梦!!!!!"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    my_write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"北京欢迎你!!!!!"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    my_write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"牛逼啊!!!!!"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'姓名\t'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'年龄\t'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'成绩\t'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'张三\t'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'30\t'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'98'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
    my_write_list<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'a.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">my_read</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>filename<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>filename<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'w+'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'你好啊!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">#写入完成,文件的指针是在最后</span>
    <span class="token comment">#seek 修改文件指针的位置</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>seek<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>read<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    my_read<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'b.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="_2530">
     </a>
     文件的复制:
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">copy</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>src<span class="token punctuation">,</span>new_path<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token comment">#边读边写操作:</span>
    <span class="token comment">#打开源文件:</span>
    file1<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>src<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'rb'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">#打开目标文件:</span>
    file2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>new_path<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'wb'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">#开始复制,边读边写</span>
    s<span class="token operator">=</span>file1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>read<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#从源文件中读取所有</span>
    file2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#向目标文件中写入所有</span>
    <span class="token comment">#关闭操作:</span>
    file2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    file1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>   <span class="token comment">#先打开的后关,后打开的先关</span>

<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    src<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'a.txt'</span>
    new_path<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'d.txt'</span>
    copy<span class="token punctuation">(</span>src<span class="token punctuation">,</span>new_path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'文件复制完毕'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="with_2551">
     </a>
     with语句:
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      称为上下文管理器,在处理文件的时候,无论是否产生异常,都能保证with语句执行完毕后关闭已经打开的文件,这个过程是自动的,无需手动操作的
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      语法结构:
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">pass</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">write_fun</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'aa.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'w'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'2022北京冬奥会,欢迎你!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">read_fun</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'aa.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'r'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> file2<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        a<span class="token operator">=</span>file2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>read<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>a<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">copy</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>src_file<span class="token punctuation">,</span>target_file<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>src_file<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'r'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> file3<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>target_file<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'w'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> file4<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            file4<span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span>file3<span class="token punctuation">.</span>read<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">#将读取的内容直接写入</span>


<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    write_fun<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    read_fun<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">#文件复制:</span>
    copy<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'aa.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'bb.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2585">
     </a>
     数据的组织维度及存储
    </h2>
    <p>
     成为数据方式或者存储方式,在python中常用的数据组织方式分为一维数据、二维数据和高维数据.
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      一纬数据
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      通常采用线性方式组织数据,一般使用Python中的列表,元组或者集合进行存储数据
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      二维数据
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      成为表格数据,由行和列组成,类似于Excel表格,在python中使用二维列表进行存储.
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      高维数据
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      使用key-value方式进行组织数据,在pyhton中使用字典进行储存数据,在pyhton中内置json模块专门处理json格式的数据
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token comment">#存储和读取一纬数据:</span>
<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">my_write</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token comment">#一维数据,可以使用列表,元组、集合,不能使用字典</span>
    lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'张三'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'李四'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'王五'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'陈六'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'郝七'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'韩子'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
    <span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'student.csv'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'w'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">','</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>join<span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>    <span class="token comment">#将列表转换成字符串</span>

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">my_read</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'student.csv'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'r'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>read<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        lst<span class="token operator">=</span>s<span class="token punctuation">.</span>split<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">','</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>


<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    my_write<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    my_read<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="json_2619">
     </a>
     json模块的常用函数
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">json<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dumps<span class="token punctuation">(</span>obj<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        将python数据类型转换成json格式过程<span class="token punctuation">,</span>编码过程
json<span class="token punctuation">.</span>loads<span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>          将json格式字符串转换成python数据类型<span class="token punctuation">,</span>解码过程
json<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dump<span class="token punctuation">(</span>obj<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>    与dumps<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>功能相同<span class="token punctuation">,</span>将转换结果存储到文件<span class="token builtin">file</span>中
json<span class="token punctuation">.</span>load<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        与loads<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>功能相同<span class="token punctuation">,</span>从文件<span class="token builtin">file</span>中读入数据
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> json
lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token string">'name'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'韩子'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'age'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">18</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'score'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">90</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token string">'name'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'张三'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'age'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">21</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'score'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">99</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token string">'name'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token string">'李四'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'age'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">19</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'score'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">89</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">]</span>

<span class="token comment">#</span>
s<span class="token operator">=</span>json<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dumps<span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">,</span>ensure_ascii<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">False</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>indent<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>   <span class="token comment">#ensure_ascii 防止乱码(正常显示中文)  indent=是缩进,美观用 JSON格式的字符串更具有可读性</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        <span class="token comment">#将lst列表编码成json字符串</span>

<span class="token comment">#解码:</span>
s1<span class="token operator">=</span>json<span class="token punctuation">.</span>loads<span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>s1<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#编码到文件中</span>
<span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'sutdent.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'w'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    json<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dump<span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>ensure_ascii<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">False</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>indent<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#从文件中解码,解码到程序</span>
<span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'student.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'r'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> file1<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    aa<span class="token operator">=</span>json<span class="token punctuation">.</span>load<span class="token punctuation">(</span>file1<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>aa<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>aa<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2652">
     </a>
     目录与文件的相关操作:
    </h2>
    <p>
     pyhton内置的与操作系统文件相关的模块,该模块中的语句的执行结果通常与操作系统有关,即有些函数的运行效果在windows操作系统和macos操作系统中不一样
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">getcwd<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>            获取当前的工作路径
listdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>       获取path路径下的文件和目录信息<span class="token punctuation">,</span>如果没有指定path<span class="token punctuation">,</span>则获取当前路径下的文件和目录信息
mkdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>         在制定路径下创建目录<span class="token punctuation">(</span>文件夹<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
makedirs<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>      创建多级目录
rmdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>         删除path下的空目录
removedirs<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>    删除多级目录
chdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>         把path设置为当前目录
walk<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>          边路目录树<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为元组<span class="token punctuation">,</span>包含所有路径名、所有目录列表和文件列表
remove<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        删除path指定的文件
rename<span class="token punctuation">(</span>old<span class="token punctuation">,</span>new<span class="token punctuation">)</span>     将old重命名为new
stat<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>          获取path指定的文件信息
starfile<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>      启动path指定的文件
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> os
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'获取当前的工作路径:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>getcwd<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>·
lst<span class="token operator">=</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>listdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'当前目录下的所有的目录以及文件:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'\n'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'指定路径下的所有的目录以及文件:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'\n'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>listdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/Users/ming/Documents/语言/C语言/test文件'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#创建目录:</span>
os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mkdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'haohao'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>      <span class="token comment">#如果要创建的文件夹存在,程序报错,报错文件已存在</span>
os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>makedirs<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'./haohao/aa/bb'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>   <span class="token comment">#创建多级目录</span>

<span class="token comment">#删除目录:</span>
os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>rmdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'./haohao'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>removedirs<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'./haohao/aa/bb'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">#如果删除的目录不存在,程序会报错!</span>

<span class="token comment">#改变当前的工作路径:</span>
os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>chdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"/User/ming"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>getcwd<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">#从这里开始,工作路径发生变化</span>

<span class="token comment">#遍历目录树,相当于递归操作:</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> dirs<span class="token punctuation">,</span>dirlst<span class="token punctuation">,</span>filelst <span class="token keyword">in</span> os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>walk<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"/Users/ming/Documents/语言"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dirs<span class="token punctuation">,</span>dirlst<span class="token punctuation">,</span>filelst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> os
<span class="token comment">#删除文件</span>
os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>remove<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'./student.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#如果要删除的程序不存在,程序报错!</span>
<span class="token comment">#重命名</span>
os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>rename<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'./student.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'newstudent.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> 

<span class="token comment">#转换时间格式</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> time 
<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">date_format</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>longtime<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
     s<span class="token operator">=</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>strftime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>localtime<span class="token punctuation">(</span>longtime<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
     <span class="token keyword">return</span> s

<span class="token comment">#获取文件信息</span>
info<span class="token operator">=</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>stat<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'./newaa.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">type</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>info<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>info<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"最近一次访问时间:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>date_format<span class="token punctuation">(</span>info<span class="token punctuation">.</span>st_atime<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'在windwos操作系统中显示的文件创建时间:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>date_format<span class="token punctuation">(</span>info<span class="token punctuation">.</span>st_ctime<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'最后一次修改时间:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>date_format<span class="token punctuation">(</span>info<span class="token punctuation">.</span>st_mtime<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"文件的大小(单位是字节):"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>info<span class="token punctuation">.</span>st_size<span class="token punctuation">)</span>


<span class="token comment">#启动路径下的文件:</span>
os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>startfile<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'终端.app'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="ospath_2719">
     </a>
     os.path模块
    </h3>
    <p>
     是os模块的子模块,也提供了一些目录或者文件的操作函数
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">abspath<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>         获取目录或文件的绝对路径
exists<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>          判断目录或文件在磁盘上是否存在<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为<span class="token builtin">bool</span>类型<span class="token punctuation">,</span>如果目录或者文件在磁盘上存在<span class="token punctuation">,</span>结果为<span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>否则为<span class="token boolean">False</span>
join<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">,</span>name<span class="token punctuation">)</span>       将目录与目录名或者文件名进行拼接<span class="token punctuation">,</span>相当于字符串中的<span class="token string">'+'</span>操作
splitext<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>            分别获取文件名和后缀名
basename<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>        从path中提取文件名
dirname<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>         从path中提取路径<span class="token punctuation">(</span>不包含文件名<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
isdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>           判断path是否具有有效路径
isfile<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>          判断<span class="token builtin">file</span>是否是有效文件
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'获取目录或者文件的绝对路径:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>abspath<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'./student.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'判断目录或者文件在磁盘上是否存在:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>exists<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'./student.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'拼接路径:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>join<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/Users/ming/Documents/语言'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'ccc.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'分割文件名和文件后缀名:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>splitext<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'b.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#元组类型,索引为0是文件名称,索引为1是文件后缀名</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'提取文件名:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>basename<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/Users/ming/Documents/语言/student.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'提取路径:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dirname<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/Users/ming/Documents/语言/student.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'判断一个路径是否为有效路径:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>isdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'/Users/ming/Documents/语言/'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">#存在就是True,不存在就是False</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2746">
     </a>
     批量创建文件:
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> random
<span class="token keyword">import</span>  os
<span class="token keyword">import</span>  os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path

<span class="token comment">#函数式编程</span>
<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">create_filename</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    filename_lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
    lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'水果'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'烟酒'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'粮油'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'肉蛋'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'蔬菜'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>  <span class="token comment">#物资的类别</span>
    code<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'0'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'1'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'2'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'3'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'4'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'5'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'6'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'7'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'8'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'9'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'A'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'B'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'C'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'D'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'E'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'F'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">3001</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        filename<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">''</span>
        <span class="token comment">#拼接文件有序号</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> i<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            filename<span class="token operator">=</span>filename<span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token string">'000'</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">elif</span> i<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            filename<span class="token operator">+=</span><span class="token string">'00'</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">elif</span> i<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token number">1000</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            filename<span class="token operator">+=</span><span class="token string">'0'</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            filename<span class="token operator">+=</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token comment">#拼接类别:</span>
        filename<span class="token operator">+=</span><span class="token string">'_'</span><span class="token operator">+</span>random<span class="token punctuation">.</span>choice<span class="token punctuation">(</span>lst<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token comment">#拼接识别码:</span>
        s<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">''</span>
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> j <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">9</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            s<span class="token operator">+=</span>random<span class="token punctuation">.</span>choice<span class="token punctuation">(</span>code<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        filename<span class="token operator">+=</span><span class="token string">'_'</span><span class="token operator">+</span>s
        filename_lst<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>filename<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> filename_lst

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">create_file</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>filename<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>filename<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">'w'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> <span class="token builtin">file</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">pass</span>

<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__ <span class="token operator">==</span> <span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token comment">#在指定的路径下创建文件:</span>
    path<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'./t'</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token keyword">not</span> os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>exists<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mkdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    lst<span class="token operator">=</span>create_filename<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>   <span class="token comment">#调用获取文件名</span>
    <span class="token comment">#开始创建文件:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> lst<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        create_file<span class="token punctuation">(</span>os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>join<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">,</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token string">'.txt'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2792">
     </a>
     批量创建文件夹
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span>  os
<span class="token keyword">import</span> os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path
<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">mkdirs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">,</span>num<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>num<span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mkdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token string">'/'</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__ <span class="token operator">==</span> <span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    path<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'./newdir'</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token keyword">not</span>  os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>path<span class="token punctuation">.</span>exists<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        os<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mkdir<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    num<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">eval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入要创建的目录个数:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    mkdirs<span class="token punctuation">(</span>path<span class="token punctuation">,</span>num<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2808">
     </a>
     进程与线程
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2809">
     </a>
     程序与进程
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      程序:英文单词为Program,是指一系列有序指令的集合,使用编程语言所编写,用于实现一定的功能 进程:启动后的程序,系统会为其分配内存空间
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2813">
     </a>
     创建进程的方式:
    </h3>
    <ul>
     <li>
      第一种创建进程的语法构:
     </li>
    </ul>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      Process(group=None,target,name,args,kwargs)
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ul>
     <li>
      参数说明:
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">group<span class="token punctuation">:</span>表示分组<span class="token punctuation">,</span>实际上不使用<span class="token punctuation">,</span>值默认为<span class="token boolean">None</span>即可
target<span class="token punctuation">:</span>表示子进程要执行的任务<span class="token punctuation">,</span>支持函数名
name<span class="token punctuation">:</span>表示子进程的名称
args<span class="token punctuation">:</span>表示调用函数的位置参数<span class="token punctuation">,</span>以元组的方式进行传递
kwargs<span class="token punctuation">:</span>表示调用函数的关键字参数<span class="token punctuation">,</span>以字典的形式进行传递
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      常用的方法和属性
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">name          当前进程实例别名<span class="token punctuation">,</span>默认为Process<span class="token operator">-</span>N
pid           当前进程对象的PID值
is_alive<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>    进程是否执行完<span class="token punctuation">,</span>没执行完结果为<span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>否则为<span class="token boolean">False</span>
join<span class="token punctuation">(</span>timeout<span class="token punctuation">)</span> 等待结束或者等待timeout秒
start<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>       启动进程
run<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>         如果没有指定target参数<span class="token punctuation">,</span>则启动进程后<span class="token punctuation">,</span>会调用父类中的run方法
terminate<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>   强制终止进程
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2840">
     </a>
     并发和并行
    </h2>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      并发:是指两个或者多个事件同一时间间隔发生,多个任务被交替轮换着执行,比如A事件是吃苹果,在吃苹果的过程中有快递员敲门让你收下快递,收快递就是事件B,那么收完快递继续吃没吃完的苹果,这就是并发
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2844">
     </a>
     进程之间的通信
    </h3>
    <p>
     进程之间可以通过队列进行通信,队列是一种先进先出的数据结构
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      创建队列的语法结构:
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">队列对象<span class="token operator">=</span>Queue<span class="token punctuation">(</span>N<span class="token punctuation">)</span> 

常用的方法<span class="token punctuation">:</span>

qsize<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>                获取当前队列包含的消息数量
empty<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>                判断队列是否为空<span class="token punctuation">,</span>为空结果为<span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>否则为<span class="token boolean">False</span>
full<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>                 判断队列是否满了<span class="token punctuation">,</span>满结果为<span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>否则为<span class="token boolean">False</span>
get<span class="token punctuation">(</span>block<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        获取队列中的一条信息<span class="token punctuation">,</span>然后从队列中移除<span class="token punctuation">,</span>block默认值为<span class="token boolean">True</span>
get_nowait<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>           相当于get<span class="token punctuation">(</span>block<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">False</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>消息队列为空时<span class="token punctuation">,</span>抛出异常
put<span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">,</span>block<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>   将item消息放入队列<span class="token punctuation">,</span>blocak默认为<span class="token boolean">True</span>
put_nowait<span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span>       相当于put<span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">,</span>block<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">False</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">from</span> multiprocessing <span class="token keyword">import</span> Queue
<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    q<span class="token operator">=</span>Queue<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列是否为空:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>empty<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列是否为满:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>full<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>put<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hello'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>put<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'world'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列是否为空:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>empty<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列是否为满:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>full<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>put<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'Python'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列是否为空:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>empty<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列是否为满:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>full<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列当中信息的个数:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>qsize<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
<span class="token comment">#出队</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列中的信息的个数:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>qsize<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#入队</span>
q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>put_nowait<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'html'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#q.put_nowait('sql') #queue.Full</span>
<span class="token comment">#q.put('sql')  不报错,会一直等待,等到队列中有空位置</span>

<span class="token comment">#遍历:</span>
<span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token keyword">not</span> q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>empty<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>qsize<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get_nowait<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">#nowait() 不等待</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列是否为空:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>empty<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'队列是否满'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>full<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"队列中消息的个数:"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>q<span class="token punctuation">.</span>qsize<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2896">
     </a>
     线程
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      线程是CPU可以调度的最小单位,被包含在进程中,是进程中实际的运作单位,一个进程中可以拥有N多个进程并发执行,而每个进程并发执行不同的任务
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     创建线程的语法结构:
    </p>
    <pre><code>t=Thread(group,target,name,args,kwargs)
参数说明:
group:创建线程对象的进程组
target:创建的线程对象所要执行的目标函数
name:创建线程对象的名称,默认为Tread-n
args:用元组以位置参数的形式传入target对应函数的参数
kwargs:用字典以关键字的形式传入target对应函数的参数
</code></pre>
    <p>
     实例:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">import</span> threading<span class="token punctuation">,</span>time
<span class="token keyword">from</span> threading <span class="token keyword">import</span> Thread
<span class="token comment">#编写函数:</span>
<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">test</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sleep<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f"线程:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>threading<span class="token punctuation">.</span>current_thread<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">正在执行</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>i<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token keyword">if</span> __name__<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'__main__'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    start<span class="token operator">=</span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>time<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"主线程开始执行"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">#线程:</span>
    lst<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>Thread<span class="token punctuation">(</span>target<span class="token operator">=</span>test<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>

    <span class="token keyword">for</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> lst<span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token comment">#遍历线程对象列表,item时Thread类型的数据类型</span>
        item<span class="token punctuation">.</span>start<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    <span class="token keyword">for</span> item <span class="token keyword">in</span> lst<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        item<span class="token punctuation">.</span>join<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">#阻塞主线程</span>
        
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f'一共耗时:</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>time<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">-</span>start<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h2>
     <a id="_2934">
     </a>
     网络编程
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="Socket_2935">
     </a>
     Socket对象的常用方法
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">bind<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>ip<span class="token punctuation">,</span>port<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>     绑定ip地址和端口
listen<span class="token punctuation">(</span>N<span class="token punctuation">)</span>           开始TCP监听<span class="token punctuation">,</span>N表示操作系统挂起的最大连接数<span class="token punctuation">,</span>取值范围<span class="token number">1</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">5</span>之间<span class="token punctuation">,</span>一般设置为<span class="token number">5</span>
accept<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>            被动接受TCP客户端连接<span class="token punctuation">,</span>阻塞式
connect<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>ip<span class="token punctuation">,</span>port<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  主动初始化TCP服务器连接
recv<span class="token punctuation">(</span>size<span class="token punctuation">)</span>          接受TCP数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>返回值为字符串类型<span class="token punctuation">,</span>size表示要接受的最大数据量 
send<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>           发送TCP数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>返回值是要发送的字节数量
sendall<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token builtin">str</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>        完整发送TCP数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>将<span class="token builtin">str</span>中的数据发送到连接的套接字<span class="token punctuation">,</span>返回之前尝试发送的所有数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>如果成功则为<span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>失败则抛出异常
recvfrom<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>          接受UDP数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>返回值为一个元组<span class="token punctuation">(</span>data<span class="token punctuation">,</span>address<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>data表示接受的数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>address表示发送数据的套接字地址
sendto<span class="token punctuation">(</span>data<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>ip<span class="token punctuation">,</span>port<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  发送UDP数据<span class="token punctuation">,</span>返回值是发送的字节数
close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>             关闭套接字
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="TCP_2950">
     </a>
     TCP编程
    </h3>
    <ul>
     <li>
      tcp服务器端编程的流程
      <br/>
      1.使用socket类创建一个套接对象
      <br/>
      2.使用bind((ip,port))方法绑定IP地址和端口号
      <br/>
      3.使用listen()方法开始TCP监听
      <br/>
      4.使用accept()方法等待客户端的连接
      <br/>
      5.使用recv()/send()方法接收/发送数据
      <br/>
      6.使用close()关闭套接字
     </li>
     <li>
      TCP客户端的编程流程
      <br/>
      1.使用socket类创建一个套接字对象
      <br/>
      2.使用connect((hots,port))设置连接的主机IP和主机设置的端口号
      <br/>
      3.使用recv()/send()方法接收/发送数据
      <br/>
      4.使用close()关闭套接字
      <br/>
      TCP编程客户端与服务器端运行有先后,先启动运行服务器端,然后启动运行客户端,连接建立后双方谁先发送数据都可以
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">服务器端<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
<span class="token keyword">from</span> socket <span class="token keyword">import</span> socket<span class="token punctuation">,</span>AF_INET<span class="token punctuation">,</span>SOCK_STREAM
<span class="token comment">#AF_INET用于Internet之间的进程通信</span>
<span class="token comment">#SOCK_STREAM #表示使用TCP协议编程</span>

<span class="token comment">#创建socket对象:</span>
server_socket<span class="token operator">=</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">(</span>AF_INET<span class="token punctuation">,</span>SOCK_STREAM<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#开始绑定ip地址和端口号:</span>
ip<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'127.0.0.1'</span>
port<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">8888</span>
server_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>bind<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>ip<span class="token punctuation">,</span>port<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#开始使用Listen()监听</span>
server_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>listen<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'服务器已经启动'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#等待客户端的连接:</span>
client_socket<span class="token punctuation">,</span>client_addr<span class="token operator">=</span>server_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>accept<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#系列解包赋值</span>

<span class="token comment">#接收来自客户端的数据:</span>
data<span class="token operator">=</span>client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>recv<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1024</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'客户端发送过来的数据为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>decode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#要求客户端发送过来的数据是使用utf-8进行编码的</span>

<span class="token comment">#关闭socket</span>
server_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>


客户端<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> socket <span class="token comment">#</span>
<span class="token comment">#创建socket对象</span>
client_socket<span class="token operator">=</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#ip地址和主机端口:</span>
ip<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'127.0.0.1'</span>
port<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">8888</span>
client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>connect<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>ip<span class="token punctuation">,</span>port<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'与服务器的连接建立成功!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#发送数据:</span>
client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>send<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'Welcome to python world'</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>encode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#关闭</span>
client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'发送完毕!结束'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     服务器端客户端多次通信
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">服务器端<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> socket
socket_obj<span class="token operator">=</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">(</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>AF_INET<span class="token punctuation">,</span> socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>SOCK_STREAM<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
socket_obj<span class="token punctuation">.</span>bind<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'127.0.0.1'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">8888</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
socket_obj<span class="token punctuation">.</span>listen<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
client_socket<span class="token punctuation">,</span>client_addr<span class="token operator">=</span>socket_obj<span class="token punctuation">.</span>accept<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#接收数据</span>
info<span class="token operator">=</span>client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>recv<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1024</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>decode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">while</span> info<span class="token operator">!=</span><span class="token string">'bye'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> info<span class="token operator">!=</span><span class="token string">' '</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'接收到的数据是:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>info<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">#准备发送的数据:</span>
    data<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入要发送的数据:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    <span class="token comment">#服务器端开始回复客户端:</span>
    client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>send<span class="token punctuation">(</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>encode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
