    <span class="token keyword">if</span> data<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'bye'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">break</span>
    info<span class="token operator">=</span>client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>recv<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1024</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>decode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">#改变变量</span>

client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
socket_obj<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

客户端<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> socket
<span class="token comment">#创建对象</span>
client_socket<span class="token operator">=</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>connect<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'127.0.0.1'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">8888</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'连接建立完成!'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment">#客户端先发送数据:</span>
info<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">''</span>
<span class="token keyword">while</span> info<span class="token operator">!=</span><span class="token string">'bye'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token comment">#准备发送的数据</span>
    send_data<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'客户端要发送的数据:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>send<span class="token punctuation">(</span>send_data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>encode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> send_data<span class="token operator">==</span><span class="token string">'bye'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">break</span> 
    
    <span class="token comment">#接受数据:</span>
    client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>recv<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1024</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>decode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
    <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'收到服务器的数据:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>info<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

client_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
    <h3>
     <a id="UDP_3056">
     </a>
     UDP编程
    </h3>
    <ul>
     <li>
      UDP服务器端:
      <br/>
      1.使用socket类创建一个套接字对象
      <br/>
      2.准备发送的数据
      <br/>
      3.定义接受方的IP地址和端口号
      <br/>
      4.使用sendto()方法发送数据
      <br/>
      5.关闭socket对象
     </li>
     <li>
      UDP客户端:
      <br/>
      1.使用socket类创建一个套接字对象
      <br/>
      2.使用bind()方法绑定IP地址和端口号
      <br/>
      3.使用recvfrom()方法接受和发送过来的数据
      <br/>
      4.关闭socket对象
      <br/>
      UDP编程接受方与发送方启动运行无先后,但是先启动的先发送, 否则数据会丢包
     </li>
    </ul>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python">服务器端<span class="token punctuation">:</span>

<span class="token keyword">from</span> socket <span class="token keyword">import</span>  socket<span class="token punctuation">,</span>AF_INET<span class="token punctuation">,</span>SOCK_DGRAM
send_socket<span class="token operator">=</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">(</span>AF_INET<span class="token punctuation">,</span>SOCK_DGRAM<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">#SOCK_DGRAM表示是UDP的数据</span>
data<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入要发送的数据:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#指定接收方的ip地址河端口:</span>
ip_port<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'127.0.0.1'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">8888</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
send_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sendto<span class="token punctuation">(</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>encode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>ip_port<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">#接收来接收方的回复数据</span>
recv_data<span class="token punctuation">,</span>addr<span class="token operator">=</span>send_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>recvfrom<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1024</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'接收到的数据为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>recv_data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>decode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
send_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

服务端<span class="token punctuation">:</span>

<span class="token keyword">from</span> socket <span class="token keyword">import</span> socket<span class="token punctuation">,</span>AF_INET<span class="token punctuation">,</span>SOCK_DGRAM
recv_socket<span class="token operator">=</span>socket<span class="token punctuation">(</span>AF_INET<span class="token punctuation">,</span>SOCK_DGRAM<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
recv_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>bind<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'127.0.0.1'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">8888</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

recv_data<span class="token punctuation">,</span>addr<span class="token operator">=</span>recv_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>recvfrom<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1024</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'接收到的数据为:'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>recv_data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>decode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

data<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token builtin">input</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'请输入要回复的数据:'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

recv_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sendto<span class="token punctuation">(</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>encode<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>addr<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

recv_socket<span class="token punctuation">.</span>close<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
